        } {in_layout = [#tpu.vpad<"none">, #tpu.vpad<"none">, #tpu.vpad<"none">, #tpu.vpad<"none">, #tpu.vpad<"none">], out_layout = [#tpu.vpad<"none">, #tpu.vpad<"none">]}
      } {in_layout = [#tpu.vpad<"none">]}
    } {in_layout = [#tpu.vpad<"none">]}
    return {in_layout = []}
  }
}
